Received response: int getfloat(double *pn)
{
    int c, sign;
    // next token or line

    while (isspace(c = getch()))
        ;

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') {
        ungetch(c);
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
    if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
        c = getch();
        if (!isdigit(c)) {
            ungetch(c);
            return 0;
        }
    }

    for (*pn = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');

    if (c == '.') {
        double power = 1.0;
        c = getch();
        for (; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
            *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
            power *= 10.0;
        }
        *pn /= power;
    }

    *pn *= sign;

    if (c != EOF)
        ungetch(c);

    return c;
}

Time taken: 3.1139838695526123 seconds
Received response: int getfloat(float *pn) {
    int c, sign;

    while (isspace(c = getch()))  // skip white space
        ;
    
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') {
        ungetch(c);  // it's not a number
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
        c = getch();
        if (!isdigit(c)) {
            ungetch(c);  // + or - not followed by a digit
            ungetch(sign == 1 ? '+' : '-');
            return 0;
        }
    }

    for (*pn = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
        *pn = *pn * 10 + (c - '0');
    
    if (c == '.')
        c = getch();
    
    float power = 1.0;

    for (; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
        *pn = *pn * 10 + (c - '0');
        power *= 10;
    }

    *pn *= sign / power;

    if (c != EOF)
        ungetch(c);

    return c;
}

    int c, sign;

    while (isspace(c = getch())) // skip white space
        ; 
    
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') {

int getfloat(float *pn)
{
  int c, sign;
  float power;

  while (isspace(c = getch())) // skip white space
    ;
  
  if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.')
  {
    ungetch(c); // it's not a number
    return 0;
  }

  sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
  
  if (c == '+' || c == '-')
    c = getch();
  
  for (*pn = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
    *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
  
  if (c == '.')
    c = getch();
  
  for (power = 1.0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
  {
    *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
    power *= 10.0;
  }
  
  *pn *= sign / power;
  
  if (c != EOF)
    ungetch(c);
  
  return c;
}

/* getch: get a (possibly pushed-back) character */
int getch(void)
{
  // code for getch function
}

/* ungetch: push character back on input */
void ungetch(int c)
{
  // code for ungetch function
}

int gettoken(void) {
    int c;
    char *p = token;

    while ((c = getch()) == ' ' || c == '\t');

    if (c == '(') {
        if ((c = getch()) == ')') {
            strcpy(token, "()");
            return type = PARENS;
        } else {
            ungetch(c);
            return type = '(';
        }
    } else if (c == '[') {
        for (*p++ = c; (*p++ = getch()) != ']';);
        *p = '\0';
        return type = BRACKETS;
    } else if (isalpha(c)) {
        for (*p++ = c; isalnum(c = getch());)
            *p++ = c;
        *p = '\0';
        ungetch(c);
        return type = NAME;
    } else
        return type = c;
}

Time taken: 3.0490362644195557 seconds
Received response: int getch(void);
void ungetch(int c);

int getfloat(float *pn) {
    int c, sign;

    while (isspace(c = getch())) {
        // skip white space
    }

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') {
        ungetch(c);  // it is not a number
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
        c = getch();
    }

    for (*pn = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
    }

    if (c == '.') {
        c = getch();
        float power = 1.0;
        for (; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
            *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
            power *= 10.0;
        }
        *pn /= power;
    }

    *pn *= sign;

    if (c != EOF) {
        ungetch(c);
    }

    return c;
}

int getch(void);
void ungetch(int c);

void getfloat(float *pn) {
    int c, sign;
    float power;

    while (isspace(c = getch())) {
        // skip white space
    }

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') {
        ungetch(c); // not a number
        return;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
        c = getch();
    }

    for (*pn = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
    }

    if (c == '.') {
        c = getch();
    }

    for (power = 1.0; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
        power *= 10.0;
    }

    *pn *= sign / power;

    if (c != EOF) {
        ungetch(c);
    }
}

int getch(void) {
    return (bufp > 0) ? buffer[--bufp] : getchar();
}

void ungetch(int c) {
    if (bufp >= 100) {
        printf("ungetch: too many characters\n");
    } else {
        buffer[bufp++] = c;
    }
}

}

void ungets(char s[])
{
    int len = strlen(s);
    for (int i = len - 1; i >= 0; i--)
    {
        ungetch(s[i]);
    }
}

int getfloat(float *pn)
{
    int c, sign;
    float power;

    while (isspace(c = getch()))
        ;

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.')
    {
        ungetch(c);
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-')
    {
        c = getch();
    }

    {

    int c;

    while ((c = getch()) == ' ' || c == '\t');

    if (c == '(' || c == ')' || c == '[' || c == ']' || c == '{' || c == '}') {
        *token++ = c;
        *token = '\0';
        return c;

            *token++ = c;

        ungetch(c);
        *token = '\0';
        return NAME;
    } else {
        *token = '\0';
        return c;
    }
}

int getfloat(double *pn) {
    int c, sign;
    double power;

    while (isspace(c = getch())) {
        /* skip white space */
    }

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') {
        ungetch(c); // it is not a number
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-') {
        c = getch();
    }

    *pn = 0.0;

    while (isdigit(c)) {
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
        c = getch();
    }

    if (c == '.') {
        c = getch();
    }

    for (power = 1.0; isdigit(c); c = getch()) {
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
        power *= 10.0;
    }

    *pn *= sign / power;

    if (c != EOF) {
        ungetch(c);
    }

    return c;
}

Received response: {
    int getch(void);
    void ungetch(int);

    int c;
    double val;

    while ((c = getch()) == ' ' || c == '\t')
        ;
    
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != '.' && c != '-' && c != '+')
    {
        return c;  // next token or line
    }

    int sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;
    if (c == '-' || c == '+')
    {
        c = getch();
    }
    
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != '.')
    {
        return c;  // next token or line
    }

    // Process integer part
    int power = 1;
    for (val = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
    {
        val = 10.0 * val + (c - '0');
    }

    // Process fraction part
    if (c == '.')
    {
        c = getch();
        for (power = 1; isdigit(c); c = getch())
        {
            val = 10.0 * val + (c - '0');
            power *= 10;
        }
    }

    val *= sign / power;

    if (c != EOF)
    {
        ungetch(c);
    }

    return val;
}

int getfloat(
                'next token or line'
                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 3.6911280155181885 seconds
Received response: int getfloat(char *line)
{
    int c;
    int sign;
    float power = 10.0;
    float val = 0.0;

    while (isspace(*line)) {
        line++;
    }

    sign = (*line == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (*line == '+' || *line == '-') {
        line++;
    }

    for (val = 0.0; isdigit(*line); line++) {
        val = 10.0 * val + (*line - '0');
    }

    if (*line == '.') {
        line++;
    }

    for (power = 1.0; isdigit(*line); line++) {
        val = val + ((*line - '0') / power);
        power *= 10.0;
    }

    if (*line == 'e' || *line == 'E') {
        line++;
        int exp_sign = (*line == '-') ? -1 : 1;

        if (*line == '+' || *line == '-') {
            line++;
        }

        int exp = 0;
        for (; isdigit(*line); line++) {
            exp = 10 * exp + (*line - '0');
        }

        while (exp > 0) {
            if (exp_sign == 1) {
                power /= 10;
            } else {
                power *= 10;
            }
            exp--;
        }
    }

    return sign * val;
}

                'next token or line'
                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 2.7613275051116943 seconds
Received response: int getfloat(float *pn)
{
    int c, sign;
    float power;

    while (isspace(c = getch()))
        ;

    if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.')
    {
        ungetch(c); // push back non-digit character
        return 0;
    }

    sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

    if (c == '+' || c == '-') // handle sign
        c = getch();

    for (*pn = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');

    if (c == '.') // handle decimal point
        c = getch();

    for (power = 1.0; isdigit(c); c = getch())
    {
        *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
        power *= 10.0;
    }

    *pn *= sign / power;

    if (c != EOF)
        ungetch(c); // push back character

    return c;
}

int getfloat(float *pn)
{
  int
                'next token or line'
                Complete the 'next token or line' part of the code in the C11 programming language. Just show your answer in place of 'next token or line'. 
                
Time taken: 5.124132871627808 seconds
Received response: int c, sign;

  while (isspace(c = getch())); // skip white space

  if (!isdigit(c) && c != EOF && c != '+' && c != '-' && c != '.') // check if the input is not a digit, not the end of file, not a sign, and not a decimal point
  {
    ungetch(c); // ungetch the character
    return 0; // not a number
  }

  sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1; // get the sign of the number
  
  if (c == '+' || c == '-') // if the first character is a sign
  {
    c = getch(); // get the next character
    if (!isdigit(c) && c != '.') // if the next character is not a digit or a decimal point
    {
      ungetch(c); // ungetch the character
      return 0; // not a number
    }
  }

  for (*pn = 0.0; isdigit(c); c = getch()) // convert the integer part of the number
  {
    *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
  }

  if (c == '.') // if there is a decimal point
  {
    c = getch(); // get the next character
    float power = 1.0;
    for (; isdigit(c); c = getch()) // convert the fractional part of the number
    {
      *pn = 10.0 * *pn + (c - '0');
      power *= 10.0;
    }
    *pn /= power;
  }

  *pn *= sign; // apply the sign to the final number

  if (c != EOF) // if c is not the end of file
  {
    ungetch(c); // ungetch the character
  }

  return c; // return the next token or line
}

    // Next token
    *pn = 0;
    return 0;
  }

  sign = (c == '-') ? -1 : 1;

  if (c == '+' || c == '-') 
  {
    c = getch();
  }

  for (*pn = 0; isdigit(c); c = getch()) 
  {
    *pn = 10 * *pn + (c - '0');
  }

  if (c == '.') 
  {
    c = getch();
    float power = 1.0;
    for (; isdigit(c); c = getch()) 
    {
      *pn = 10 * *pn + (c - '0');
      power *= 10;
    }
    
    *pn /= power;
  }

  *pn *= sign;

  if (c != EOF) 
  {
    ungetch(c);
  }

  return c;
}

    ungetch(c);
